				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Artaserse (Hasse, Johann Adolph)				</h1>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 Acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Opera_seria&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Opera seria</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Theatrical_Works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Theatrical Works</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Librettos&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Librettos</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Writings&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Writings</a></span>; <th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1730-02-11 in Venice: <a href="/wiki/Chronology_of_productions_at_Teatro_San_Giovanni_Grisostomo" title="Chronology of productions at Teatro San Giovanni Grisostomo">Teatro San Giovanni Grisostomo</a> <span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">A</span><br />1740-09-09 in Dresden: Hofoper (<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Opernhaus_am_Zwinger" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:Opernhaus am Zwinger">Opernhaus am Zwinger</a>) <span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">B</span><br />1760-01-20 in Naples: <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Teatro_di_San_Carlo" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:en:Teatro di San Carlo">Teatro di San Carlo</a> <span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">C</span> <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd>Venice Production
<dl><dd>Filippo Giorgi (Artaserse)<br /><a href="/wiki/Francesca_Cuzzoni" title="Francesca Cuzzoni" class="mw-redirect">Francesca Cuzzoni</a> (Mandane)<br />Nicola Grimaldi (Artabano)<br /><a href="/wiki/Carlo_Broschi" title="Carlo Broschi" class="mw-redirect">Carlo Broschi</a>, aka Farinelli (Arbace)<br />Maria Maddalena Pieri (Semira)<br />Castore Antonio Castori (Meabise)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd>Dresden Production
<dl><dd>Filippo Giorgi (Artaserse)<br />Faustina Bordoni-Hasse (Mandane)<br />Domenico Annibali (Artabano)<br />Ventura Rocchetti (Arbace)<br />Sofia Denner (Semira)<br />Giovanni Bindi (Megabise)</span>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

Boldoni<br /><span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">B</span> and <span style="background:#c2c8cd;color:#003d70;padding:0 4px">C</span> <a href="/wiki/Category:Metastasio,_Pietro" title="Category:Metastasio, Pietro">Pietro Metastasio</a> (1698-1782)

<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>According to this <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Artaserse" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Artaserse">Wikipedia</a> article, Hasse also contributed to a 1734 pastiche of Artaserse, along with Attilio Ariosti, Nicola Porpora and Riccardo Broschi. It is unknown whether the contribution was pre-existing arias from this opera.  See also <i><a href="/wiki/Artaserse_(Broschi,_Riccardo)" title="Artaserse (Broschi, Riccardo)">Artaserse</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Category:Broschi,_Riccardo" title="Category:Broschi, Riccardo">Broschi</a>, <i><a href="/wiki/Artaserse_(Ariosti,_Attilio)" title="Artaserse (Ariosti, Attilio)">Artaserse</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Category:Ariosti,_Attilio" title="Category:Ariosti, Attilio">Ariosti</a>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Artaserse_(Porpora,_Nicola_Antonio)" title="Artaserse (Porpora, Nicola Antonio)">Artaserse</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Category:Porpora,_Nicola_Antonio" title="Category:Porpora, Nicola Antonio">Porpora</a>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
